        <div id="js-article-text" class="article-text wide">
            <h1>Indenial.com: Website allows Hillary Clinton supporters to pretend to live in alternate universe where the Democratic candidate won </h1>      
      <ul class="mol-bullets-with-font"><li class=""><strong>HillarybeatTrump.org brands itself as 'News from the real America where the majority rules'</strong></li><li class=""><strong>The site publishes fake news about a world in where Clinton is the 45th president</strong></li><li class=""><strong>Articles report on Hillary's approval rates rising to '89 per cent'</strong></li><li class=""><strong>Other headlines include: 'Clinton raises taxes, Koch brothers flee America'</strong></li><li class=""><strong>The site states the views are satirical, but also calls itself a 'movement' </strong></li></ul><p class="author-section byline-plain">By

<a href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Karen+Ruiz+For+Dailymail.com" class="author" rel="nofollow">Karen Ruiz For Dailymail.com</a>


</p><p class="byline-section"><span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-published">
  <span class="article-timestamp-label">Published:</span>
  16:23 EST, 23 February 2017
</span>
 | <span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-updated">
  <span class="article-timestamp-label">Updated:</span>
  18:45 EST, 23 February 2017
</span>

</p><div itemprop="articleBody"><p class="mol-para-with-font">A pro-Hillary Clinton website allows the Democratic candidate's supporters to pretend to live in an alternate universe where she won the 2016 presidential election. </p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" class="" rel="nofollow" href="http://www.hillarybeattrump.org/">HillarybeatTrump.org</a> brands itself as 'New from the real America where the majority rules,' alluding to her victory in the popular vote in November.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">The website description says: 'In the midst of a Constitutional crisis, this is our response. Long live the true president, Hillary Rodham Clinton.' </p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group">    <div class="mol-img">
    <img id="i-8c44b4d6ca2f7874" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/02/23/20/3D96261600000578-0-image-a-36_1487883462076.jpg" height="404" width="634" alt="HillarybeatTrump.org brands itself as 'News from the real America where the majority rules' and as a response to a 'Constitutional crisis' " class="blkBorder img-share"/>
    <noscript>
      <img id="i-8c44b4d6ca2f7874" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/02/23/20/3D96261600000578-0-image-a-36_1487883462076.jpg" height="404" width="634" alt="HillarybeatTrump.org brands itself as 'News from the real America where the majority rules' and as a response to a 'Constitutional crisis' " class="blkBorder img-share"/>
    </noscript>

</div></div><div class="clear"></div><p class="imageCaption">Hillary 2016? The site publishes satirical articles in world where Clinton is the 45th president of the United States </p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font">The 'news' site states it 'fearlessly and satirically' covers issues including: the Alt-Right, 'Failed Candidate Trump', male epiphanies, the first gentlemen, Beyonce, and healthcare.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">The fantasy website states it is based on satire, but also calls itself a movement and allows readers to subscribe to its newsletter. The authors of the site are not identified, but also have ownership of the <a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" class="" rel="nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/potushill">Twitter</a> and <a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" class="" rel="nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/hillarybeattrump/">Facebook</a> sites.</p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group"><div class="splitLeft"><div class="mol-img" style="height: auto;">

<script type="text/javascript">
    DM.later('bundle', function(){
        var n = 0;
        var taboola_every_n = 10;
        var taboola_counter = 10;

        var addTaboola = function (node){
            var id = "taboola-stream-thumbnails-" + (++n);
            var taboola_node = '<div id="' + id + '" style="min-height: 280px;"></div>';
            $(node).before(taboola_node);

            window._taboola = window._taboola || [];
            _taboola.push({
                mode: 'thumbnails-b',
                container: id,
                placement: "Stream Thumbnails " + n});
        };

        DM.has('infinite-list', 'InfiniteList', {
url: '/api/infinite-list.html?channelShortName=news&pageSize=10',
            total: 12.0,
            from: 0,
            onAfterAppend: function (container){
                var items = $(container).children('div');
                if(!taboola_every_n){
                    return;
                }

                items.each(function (){
                    if (taboola_counter == 0){
                        addTaboola(this);
                        taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;
                    }
                    else {
                        taboola_counter--;
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    });
</script>
